   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of minimum driving ages</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">
       Wikipedia list article
      </div> 
      <p>The <b>minimum driving age</b> is the minimum age at which a person may obtain a <a href="/wiki/Driver%27s_licence" class="mw-redirect" title="Driver's licence">driver's licence</a> to lawfully drive a motor vehicle on public roads. That age is determined by and for each jurisdiction and is most commonly set at 18 years of age, but learner drivers may be permitted on the road at an earlier age under supervision. Before reaching the minimum age for a driver's licence or anytime afterwards, the person wanting the licence would normally be tested for driving ability and knowledge of road rules before being issued with a licence, provided he or she is above the minimum driving age. Countries with the lowest driving ages (17 and below) are Canada, El Salvador, Iceland, Israel, Malaysia, Australia, New Zealand, the Philippines, the United Kingdom (mainland), United States and Zimbabwe. In some jurisdictions in the United States and Canada, drivers can be as young as 14 (with parental supervision). </p>
      <p>Most jurisdictions recognise driver's licences issued by another jurisdiction, which may result in a young person who obtains a licence in a jurisdiction with a low minimum driving age being permitted to drive in a jurisdiction which normally has a higher driving age. A notable exception to this is the United States, where many states ban drivers below their minimum driving age, even if they hold permits or licences issued by another state. </p>
      <p>The minimum age may vary depending on vehicle type. This list refers to the minimum driving age for a light motor vehicle (typically under 3500&nbsp;kg gross vehicle mass) or motorcycle, where noted. </p>

      <table class="wikitable sortable">

        <tr>

         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> </td> 
         <td style="text-align:center;">17 </td> 
         <td>21 is the minimum age to drive a truck, bus or <a href="/wiki/Emergency_vehicle" title="Emergency vehicle">emergency vehicle</a>. 16 is the minimum age to drive a <a href="/wiki/Moped" title="Moped">moped</a> (without passengers). Parental approval is necessary for any license issued to any individual aged under 18.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> </td>

      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:552px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Driving_age_Europe.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Driving_age_Europe.svg/550px-Driving_age_Europe.svg.png" decoding="async" width="550" height="421" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Driving_age_Europe.svg/825px-Driving_age_Europe.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Driving_age_Europe.svg/1100px-Driving_age_Europe.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="680" data-file-height="520"></a>

         <br>
         <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r981673959">.mw-parser-output .legend{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}.mw-parser-output .legend-color{display:inline-block;min-width:1.25em;height:1.25em;line-height:1.25;margin:1px 0;text-align:center;border:1px solid black;background-color:transparent;color:black}.mw-parser-output .legend-text{}</style>
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0026FF; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum driving age is 18

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Oceania">Oceania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_minimum_driving_ages&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Oceania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

         <td style="text-align:center;">18 (VIC) 17 (All other States) 16½ years (NT) </td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           See also: <a href="/wiki/Driving_licence_in_Australia" class="mw-redirect" title="Driving licence in Australia">Driving licence in Australia</a>
          </div>Learner drivers may drive under qualified supervision from the minimum age set in each state or territory. </td>

         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg/23px-Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg/35px-Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg/46px-Flag_of_New_Zealand.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a> </td> 
         <td style="text-align:center;">16 </td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           See also: <a href="/wiki/Driving_licence_in_New_Zealand" class="mw-redirect" title="Driving licence in New Zealand">Driving licence in New Zealand</a>
          </div>The minimum age to obtain a car or motorcycle learner licence which allows driving under supervision is 16. The minimum possible age to obtain a full licence, without any supervision or conditions, is 17½ years if a driver completes an advanced driving course.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup> Without an advanced driving course, the minimum age is 18, the same as a heavy vehicle licence.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>
